  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_06e446ff-e257-45a6-bbe1-5c01c0dbf8fe'
      });
    }

  <span id="freeText3646472887474797355" style="display:none"><strong>Unleash the power of your Soul! Is Heaven real, accessible and ready to help us discover our life path?</strong><br /><br />WHAT IF YOU COULD:<br /><br /><br />Feel like <em>you</em> are driving your life, not the other way around? Tap into the power of heaven? Get on the path to living the purpose and passion for the rest of your life? That's exactly what happened to Clifford Michaels, a Wall Street investment advisor, who never believed the "afterlife" existed. Everything changed after a brush with kidney cancer that set him on a reluctant path of spiritual discovery. He first denied, then acknowledged, and finally embraced and <em>interacted</em> with "heavenly" forces he realized want to help <em>all</em> of us find our ideal path in life.<br /><br />The result? <em>Harnessing Heaven</em>, the book that shows you how to actually tap into the power of Heaven, as part of a dynamic process of self-discovery.<br /><br />In <em>Harnessing Heaven</em>, you'll discover:<br /><br /><br /><strong>The Seven Principles for Clarifying Your Life's Purpose</strong> Spirituality and a higher plane of guidance, grace and wisdom. The divine teachings we need to know in order to evolve in this life How to determine your purpose and passion for the rest of your life. A crash course in understanding the dynamic reality we live in. How to raise your energy vibration for health and listen to heaven. Combining teachings from heaven, and down-to-earth, actionable lessons and strategies, <em>Harnessing Heaven</em> and its core "Seven Principles" opens the door to discovering and mapping out your ideal life path--with confidence, conviction and passion!</span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_2186887537" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2186887537" />
    <a title="Novel Addiction" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/73909712-novel-addiction"><img alt="Novel Addiction" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/images/nophoto/user/c_111x148.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2186887537?book_show_action=true">Nov 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Novel Addiction" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Novel Addiction" href="/user/show/73909712-novel-addiction">Novel Addiction</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2186887537" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1816897693624162616">Clifford Michaels is a man with a mission to discover the meaning of life and why we are here as well as what happens when we die and whether there is an afterlife or not. He details in this great book of his his days of being a fresh-out-of-college individual who landed a job located on Wall Street in New York City to being a married man with an equally hardworking wife to the time they bought a house in the suburbs just outside of NYC while commuting to work in the city. He tells of how he cam</span>
  <span id="freeText1816897693624162616" style="display:none">Clifford Michaels is a man with a mission to discover the meaning of life and why we are here as well as what happens when we die and whether there is an afterlife or not. He details in this great book of his his days of being a fresh-out-of-college individual who landed a job located on Wall Street in New York City to being a married man with an equally hardworking wife to the time they bought a house in the suburbs just outside of NYC while commuting to work in the city. He tells of how he came to find out about the world of spiritual mediums and how they helped him seek answers to his questions about heaven and everything about it that intrigues him. Michaels’ wish for us the readers of his book is that “after completing it we will have a better understanding of who we are and why we are here and where we fit in the cycle of life. He also hopes that this book will be a valuable tool for us all in inspiring us to make positive changes and contributions that could have a beneficial ripple effect around the world…”<br /><br />By the time Michaels was thirty he had earned a good amount of financial capital that he decided to start his own financial planning firm and use his acquired knowledge to work with individuals and private businesses. In other words, he is a self-made man with a good head on his shoulders who was very diligent in meeting his goals and in taking care of his little family. He was very interested in looking for new ways to prosper more and to feel that all his hard work may well have a meaning that will propel him and his family to elevated levels of happiness, happy with their lives and where life has taken them. He says also that he is not a religious man and does not belong to an established religion but he “hoped that if there was a higher power that is watching over him, it would aid him in being successful.”<br /><br />I found this book to be quite an experience as I myself am a Catholic and believed wholeheartedly that my own happiness comes from my faith but that this man who is not a churchgoer is getting it in life and is on the get-go. It intrigues me because that’s how mysterious life is. I recommend this book to all those who do not belong to any religion but at the same time has faith in a higher being because they will relate to it more than I did. I also think it’s very admirable to know that there are people out there who have concerns with where they are headed to in life without any awareness of such notable religious figures as Jesus Christ, Buddha, or Muhammad who are well-known for their teachings on how to get by in life. It makes me regard Clifford Michaels as an individual who is humble just by his thinking that there must be a higher power out there and that from such comes success and happiness. I must suggest to the non-churchgoer to buy this book because Michaels has a great idea on how to achieve your financial goals that will bring about contentment in your life thus bringing about peace and bliss in your journey as well as those around you witnessing your happiness.<br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1816897693624162616" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2154767521" />
    <a title="Page After Page" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/72617110-page-after-page"><img alt="Page After Page" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1517234316p2/72617110.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2154767521?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Page After Page" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Page After Page" href="/user/show/72617110-page-after-page">Page After Page</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2154767521" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3783028329811211044">Harnessing Heaven: How One Reluctant Wall-Streeter Tapped the Power of the Hereafter by Clifford Michaels is a first hand account of one man's life and his absolute spiritual transformation. In the early 1980's the author became a successful Wall Street trader, making the requisite amount of money to afford a cushy lifestyle and even moved to the country outside of New York city to escape some of the inherent tension in the city. In particular after living through 9/11 and the aftermath, the aut</span>
  <span id="freeText3783028329811211044" style="display:none">Harnessing Heaven: How One Reluctant Wall-Streeter Tapped the Power of the Hereafter by Clifford Michaels is a first hand account of one man's life and his absolute spiritual transformation. In the early 1980's the author became a successful Wall Street trader, making the requisite amount of money to afford a cushy lifestyle and even moved to the country outside of New York city to escape some of the inherent tension in the city. In particular after living through 9/11 and the aftermath, the author wanted to escape and re-visit life. Life is going rather well, until Michaels' discovers he has kidney cancer, and from there in addition to trying to heal himself physically, he embarks on a spiritual awakening. He explores the writings and works of Edgar Cayce and attends various groups with mediums. These experiences lead him to have an epiphany of sorts, and help him to further explore his own belief system, and try to understand his own perceptions of the hereafter. This is a heartfelt, personal story, that proves to be motivational and spiritual at the same time. This book is a great reminder that we always don't have control over our lives, that life and every day is precious, and to not be afraid of the unknown. Strongly recommend for an enriching and expansive reading experience.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3783028329811211044" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer18064108378256120380">I found this a pretty interesting book, even as a non-religious, non-spiritual person. Apart from the references to heaven, God etc. the bulk of the text essentially concerns positivity, openness and change and applies these to meditative and spiritual practices.  <br/>Clifford Michaels muses on the meaning of life, why we are here, what happens when life ends and whether there’s an afterlife. The book ‘chronicles (the author’s) journey into the world of the spiritual unknown’ from the perspective of</span>
  <span id="freeText18064108378256120380" style="display:none">I found this a pretty interesting book, even as a non-religious, non-spiritual person. Apart from the references to heaven, God etc. the bulk of the text essentially concerns positivity, openness and change and applies these to meditative and spiritual practices.  <br />Clifford Michaels muses on the meaning of life, why we are here, what happens when life ends and whether there’s an afterlife. The book ‘chronicles (the author’s) journey into the world of the spiritual unknown’ from the perspective of a sceptic. <br /><br />Michaels documents his experiences living through life threatening illness, working in Wall Street on the New York Stock Exchange, the stress of the 9/11 World Trade Centre attack and also his wife’s infertility treatment. Against this personal backdrop he discusses the confusion and uncertainty of spiritual and religious belief. <br /><br />He gives guidelines and advice about how to change our beliefs and behavior for the better. This book offered more than it first appeared to and was an easy and enjoyable read too. <br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7713030079851878293">‘Harnessing Heaven’ is Clifford Michaels one man account of his own personal development. After stressful life experiences including cancer, infertility and the 2001 terrorist attack on the World Trade Center prompted the author to look for reason and answers to fundamental questions, he found spiritualism, in the form of group Circles, hosted by a medium. <br/><br/>The author avoids inflicting readers with tedious life-affirming nonsense, in favour of a well-balanced selection of anecdotes, quotes, refer</span>
  <span id="freeText7713030079851878293" style="display:none">‘Harnessing Heaven’ is Clifford Michaels one man account of his own personal development. After stressful life experiences including cancer, infertility and the 2001 terrorist attack on the World Trade Center prompted the author to look for reason and answers to fundamental questions, he found spiritualism, in the form of group Circles, hosted by a medium. <br /><br />The author avoids inflicting readers with tedious life-affirming nonsense, in favour of a well-balanced selection of anecdotes, quotes, references and teachings that amount to a book that is easy to digest, understand and learn from. Readers don’t have to wade through page after page of miracles or proof of a higher power, just the author’s journey, laid out simply and logically. I say logically even coming from the point of view of a sceptic (as the author claims he was too). An interesting read with much food for thought. <br /><br /><br /></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('bKTJQLix42WHXg8kq+JFUeC7LPUlnn+9OTorpLz5ZZIppyyh+efpjBPWcRReXqnUKFjto9bR8nKfANrBYLtYFQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34146782-my-grandmother-s-hands"><img alt="My Grandmother&#39;s Hands: Racialized Trauma and the Mending of Our Bodies and Hearts" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1489155853l/34146782._SX98_.jpg" />

      var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_34146782'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/34146782-my-grandmother-s-hands?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">My Grandmother&#39;s Hands: Racialized Trauma and the Mending of Our Bodies and Hearts<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/8394042.Resmaa_Menakem?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Resmaa Menakem<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.45 avg rating &mdash; 1,957 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2017\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer15032348325443604688\">The body is where our instincts reside and where we fight, flee, or freeze, and it endures the trauma inflicted by the ills that plague society. In this groundbreaking work, therapist Resmaa Menakem examines the damage caused by racism in America fro<\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText15032348325443604688\" style=\"display:none\">The body is where our instincts reside and where we fight, flee, or freeze, and it endures the trauma inflicted by the ills that plague society. In this groundbreaking work, therapist Resmaa Menakem examines the damage caused by racism in America from the perspective of body-centered psychology. He argues this destruction will continue until Americans learn to heal the generational anguish of white supremacy, which is deeply embedded in all our bodies. Our collective agony doesn\'t just affect African Americans. White Americans suffer their own secondary trauma as well. So do blue Americans—our police.\n\nMy Grandmother\'s Hands is a call to action for all of us to recognize that racism is not about the head, but about the body, and introduces an alternative view of what we can do to grow beyond our entrenched racialized divide.\n\n\n\nPaves the way for a new, body-centered understanding of white supremacy—how it is literally in our blood and our nervous system.\n\n\nOffers a step-by-step solution—a healing process—in addition to incisive social commentary.\n\nResmaa Menakem, MSW, LICSW, is a therapist with decades of experience currently in private practice in Minneapolis, MN, specializing in trauma, body-centered psychotherapy, and violence prevention. He has appeared on the Oprah Winfrey Show and Dr. Phil as an expert on conflict and violence. Traditionally, it was considered sunrise was the beginning of a day, yet in this formal world, a day begins at midnight and ends at the same time.
